 bisisiai kii chayansmiti ke adhyaksh em
 s
 ke
 Prasad recently raised questions about the future of former India captain Mahendra Singh Dhoni
 lekin team ke head coach ravi shastri prasad se alag raay rakhte hai
 Shastri gave a statement in favor of Dhoni saying that given his current form, the team management cannot think of removing him from the team
 dhoni ne srilanka daure par jabardast form kaa parichay dete hue 82
 He scored 162 runs at 23 strike rate and also showed great agility behind the wicket
 dhoni is daure par vanade main 100 stamping karne vaale pehle wicketiper bhi bane
 Ravi Shastri told a private channel that Dhoni has both fitness and form and the team will need him in the 2019 World Cup
 shastri ne dhoni kii tulana mahaan ballebaaj sunil gavaskar, sachin tendulkar or olerounder kapil dev ke saath karte hue kaha ki unki uplabdhiyon kaa sammaan karnaa jaruri he
 Shastri said, "where will you find a legend like Dhoni? Dhoni is equal to Sunil Gavaskar, Sachin Tendulkar and Kapil Dev
 hamen unki uplabdhiyon kaa sammaan karnaa chahie
 "shastri praised Dhoni's performance in Sri Lanka and said he still had a lot of cricket left in him
 shastri ne kaha, "kisi khilaadi kaa moolyankan uske maujuuda form or fitness ke aadhaar par hota he or dhoni ke paas ye donon hai
 If you look at his wicketkeeping, he is the best in ODI cricket
 unki fitness gajab kii he, unhone srilanka main bahut acchhee ballebaaji kii or main aapako bataa duun ki srilanka main aapane jo dekha tha wo mahaj ek trailor dekha tha
 Now wait for the film
 "shastri ne kaha, "agar dhoni isi tarah se khelte rahete hai, tab to koi vajah nahin ki vah 2019 world cap ke liye team main nahin honge
 You cannot imagine a team without Dhoni

 The company priced it 13
 28 lakh rupee (eks-showrooms, dilli) rakhi thi
 Despite being a very powerful bike, Versys continued to face challenges in India with the Triumph Tiger 800, Honda Africa Twin, BMW r 1200 GS Adventure and Ducati Multistrada 950
 company kaa dhyaan abdhersys-x 300 or Versys 650par rahegaa or company inke cells badhaane ke liye kaam karegi
 The remaining stock of the Versys 1000 was sold only last year
 Versys 1000 main 1043cc in line four silinder ingine maujuud he
 This engine generates power of 118bhp and pickup torque of 102nm
 transmishan ke liye ise 6-speed gearbox se joda gaya he
 The Versys 1000 weighs 239 kg and its seat height is 845mm
 fitures kii baat karen to is bike main semi-digital instrument consol diya gaya he

 raashtrapati ne 4 nae jajon ko di manzoorisupreme court main ab honge 34 jajrashtrapati ramnath kovind ne supreme court main chaar nae jajon kii niyukti ko manjuuri di he
 With the appointment of new judges, the number of judges has increased to 34 in the Supreme Court
 nae jajon main justise ramsubramanyan, justise krishna murari, justise es rabindra bhatta or justise hrishikesh roy ko raashtrapati ne niyukti di he
 Earlier, the number of judges in the Supreme Court was 31
 centre sarkaar ne haal main badhaakar 34 kar di thi, jisamen chif justise bhi shaamil hai
 The Supreme Court Collegium had sent the recommendation of the name of Himachal Pradesh High Court Chief Justice Ram Subramanian, Justice Krishna Murari of Punjab and Haryana High Court, r Ravindra Bhatt of Rajasthan High Court and Hrishikesh Roy from Kerala High Court
 sarkaar ne in naamon ko manjuur kar liya tha, jisko raashtrapati ne manjuuri de di he
 Earlier this month, President Ram Nath Kovind signed a bill to increase the number of judges from 31 to 34 in the Supreme Court
 raashtrapati kovind ke hastakshar ke baad is sambandh main 12 agast ko rajptr bhi jari kar diya gaya
